[Wendy](/wiki/Wendy "Wendy")[Don't Starve](/wiki/Wendy/Don%27t_Starve "Wendy/Don't Starve")[DST](/wiki/Wendy/Don%27t_Starve_Together "Wendy/Don't Starve Together")**Quotes**[Gallery](/wiki/Wendy/Gallery "Wendy/Gallery")

| --- | --- |
|  | This article is **incomplete** *because of the evil sabotage by [Maxwell](/wiki/Maxwell/NPC "Maxwell/NPC")...*. Please help to [improve the article](https://dontstarve.fandom.com/wiki/Wendy/Quotes?action=edit), or discuss the issue with the community on the [comment section](/wiki/Wendy#WikiaArticleComments "Wendy"). |

 https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/dont-starve-game/images/c/c8/Wendy talking.png/revision/latest?cb=20130216120327 

That's my twin sister, Abigail.

 

**“**Everything dies.**”**

–[Wendy](/wiki/Wendy "Wendy")

This page lists [Wendy's](/wiki/Wendy "Wendy") [Quotes](/wiki/Character_quotes "Character quotes") which are spoken when the player examines an in-game item or object. The player can alt-click items and objects to examine them.

### https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/dont-starve-game/images/4/4d/Icon Tools.png/revision/latest?cb=20210625093434Tools[]

#### Base Game[]

* AxeAxe- "An instrument for industry and murder."
* Luxury AxeLuxury Axe- "At least I can kill trees with style."
* ShovelShovel- "What terrible secrets might I uncover?"
* Regal ShovelRegal Shovel- "At least I can dig with style."
* PickaxePickaxe- "So that I may penetrate the earth itself."
* Opulent PickaxeOpulent Pickaxe- "At least I can smash rocks with style."
* RazorRazor- "This is just for shaving."
* HammerHammer- "Oh that I may crush the world."
* PitchforkPitchfork- "What a devilish tool!"
* Feather PencilFeather Pencil- "M...maybe I'll doodle something... When no one's looking."
* BrushBrush- "Oh, to rid the world of fluff."
* SaddleSaddle- "As if it wasn't already burdened by the yoke of life..."
* War SaddleWar Saddle- "Oh, how we bend creatures to our ill intent."
* Glossamer SaddleGlossamer Saddle- "Too much whimsy gives me indigestion."
* SaddlehornSaddlehorn- "I'm only taking back what's mine."
* Salt LickSalt Lick- "The beasts crave it..."

* ShearsShears- "Can it shear my heart?"

#### Don't Starve Together[]

* Luxury AxeLuxury Axe- "One might as well kill trees with style."
* ShovelShovel- "What terrible secrets might be uncovered with this?"
* Regal ShovelRegal Shovel- "One might as well can dig with style."
* PickaxePickaxe- "That the earth itself might be penetrated."
* Opulent PickaxeOpulent Pickaxe- "One might as well smash rocks with style."
* HammerHammer- "This hammer does not create... it only destroys..."
* Pocket ScalePocket Scale- "What is the weight of my actions?"
* Garden HoeGarden Hoe- "I must prepare the seeds for their burial."
* Splendid Garden HoeSplendid Garden Hoe- "One might as well garden in style."
* Watering CanWatering Can- "I could water the ground well enough with my tears."
* Watering CanWaterfowl CanWatering Can and Waterfowl Can (empty)- "Dry as a bone..."
* Waterfowl CanWaterfowl Can- "What an odd looking watering can."
* Beefalo BellBeefalo Bell- "Alas, not a death knell."

#### Don't Starve Together[]

* Fire PitFire Pit (upon being built, generic)- "A flame to keep the horrors at bay."
* Fire PitFire Pit (high)- "This fire burns with passion!"
* Fire PitFire Pit (normal)- "It's a comfort."
* Fire PitFire Pit (low)- "It's losing the will to go on."
* Fire PitFire Pit (embers)- "Don't give up, little flame!"
* Fire PitFire Pit (out)- "This can be rekindled, unlike my heart."
* Endothermic FireEndothermic Fire PitEndothermic Fire and Fire Pit (out)- "That is not a good sign."
* Mushlight BuildMushlight (off)- "Oh look... A mushroom..."
* MushlightMushlight (on)- "Abigail would have thought this was... pretty..."

## Placeholder Trivia[]

* When she examines a [Crow](/wiki/Crow "Crow"), she says "Take thy beak from out my heart". This is a reference to a famous poem *[The Raven](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Raven "wikipedia:The Raven")* by Edgar Allan Poe.
* When she examines a [Pond](/wiki/Pond "Pond"), she says "Ophelia, are you down there?" This is a reference to the fictional character in Shakespeare's *"Hamlet"* who committed suicide by drowning herself.
* Her quote for a Toy Cobra ("To frolic, to play, no more.") is a reference to Hamlet's [famous soliloquy](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/To_be,_or_not_to_be "wikipedia:To be, or not to be") ("To die, to sleep—No more—and by a sleep to say we end the heartache and the thousand natural shocks that flesh is heir to.")
* Her line for being unable to construct the Celestial Portal due to having no materials ("Nothing comes of nothing.") could be a reference to the philosophical expression of *[ex nihilo nihil fit](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nothing_comes_from_nothing "wikipedia:Nothing comes from nothing")*, or it could refer to the line said in *[King Lear](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King_Lear "wikipedia:King Lear")*, given Wendy's tendency to reference Shakespeare.
* When she examines a [Bee Hive](/wiki/Bee_Hive "Bee Hive"), she says "A wretched hive of scum and pollen". This is a reference to *Star Wars*, "A wretched hive of scum and villainy".
* Wendy's examination quote for a Potter's Wheel with material placed on it ("Abigail... You be Death, I'll be the Sculptor...") is a reference to the sculpture *[Death and the Sculptor](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Death_and_the_Sculptor "wikipedia:Death and the Sculptor")*, a memorial for a pair of siblings.
* Her examination quote for a Boarilla ("You shall fall.") is probably a reference to [King Kong](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King_Kong "wikipedia:King Kong"), given the Boarilla's appearance and attributes.
* When she examines a [Rabbit Hole](/wiki/Rabbit_Hole "Rabbit Hole"), she says "I'm too big to fall in there". This is a reference to *[Alice's Adventures in Wonderland](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alice%27s_Adventures_in_Wonderland "wikipedia:Alice's Adventures in Wonderland")* by Charles Lutwidge Dodgson, better known under his pseudonym Lewis Carroll.
  + Her quote for the Suspicious Marble (Knight) ("Off with his head! Heehee.") is also a reference to this, specifically to the Queen of Hearts, who has a tendency to order beheadings.
  + Wendy's [Mushy Cake](/wiki/Mushy_Cake "Mushy Cake") quote is a reference to the caterpillar's mushroom in Chapter 5.
* When she examines a [Pig Head](/wiki/Pig_Head "Pig Head"), she says, "Kill the pig! Spill his blood!"; this is a reference to a chant the kids yell in the novel *[Lord of the Flies](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lord_of_the_Flies "wikipedia:Lord of the Flies")* by William Golding.
* When she examines a [Spear](/wiki/Spear "Spear"), she says "I have become the destroyer of worlds", which is a reference to the quote: "Now I have become death, the destroyer of worlds" from the *[Bhagavad Gita](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bhagavad_Gita "wikipedia:Bhagavad Gita")*. The most known instance of the quote comes from physicist J. Robert Oppenheimer, who said those words when the first atomic bomb was detonated.
* When she examines [MacTusk](/wiki/MacTusk "MacTusk"), she says "An old man, of the sea", which is a reference to the novel *[The Old Man and the Sea](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Old_Man_and_the_Sea "wikipedia:The Old Man and the Sea")* by Ernest Hemingway.
* When she examines a dead bird inside the [Birdcage](/wiki/Birdcage "Birdcage"), she says "That... is an ex-bird", which is most likely a reference to a "Monty Python's Flying Circus" skit titled "Dead Parrot".
* When she examines the [Wardrobe](/wiki/Wardrobe "Wardrobe"), she says "It reminds me of a story I read with Abigail.", which may be a reference to *[The Lion, the Witch, and the Wardrobe](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Lion,_the_Witch_and_the_Wardrobe "wikipedia:The Lion, the Witch and the Wardrobe")*, the first published book in *[The Chronicles of Narnia](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Chronicles_of_Narnia "wikipedia:The Chronicles of Narnia")* book series.
* When Wendy examines Ice Cream, she says "Ice Cream could never replace Abigail". This is likely a reference to it replenishing the exact amount of [Sanity](/wiki/Sanity "Sanity") that summoning Abigail costs.
* Wendy's quote for [The Lazy Explorer](/wiki/The_Lazy_Explorer "The Lazy Explorer") is a reference to the idea that realistic teleportation would not work as it does in movies or video games. In the real world, scientists speculate that a teleporter would destroy the subject (by taking them apart at the atomic level, effectively killing them) at the first location and then create an exact copy at the new location.
* Her examination quote for the Salt Pond in the Gorge event ("Water, water, everywhere...") is a reference to [Samuel Taylor Coleridge](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Samuel_Taylor_Coleridge "wikipedia:Samuel Taylor Coleridge")'s poem *[The Rime of the Ancient Mariner](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Rime_of_the_Ancient_Mariner "wikipedia:The Rime of the Ancient Mariner")* (a modern version of the full line being "Water, water, everywhere, but not a drop to drink.").
* Her examination quote for an Old Coin ("I shall put them on my eyes when I die.") is a reference to the tradition of placing coins on the eyes of decreased to pay the ferryman.
* When she examines The [Eye of the Tiger Shark](/wiki/Eye_of_the_Tiger_Shark "Eye of the Tiger Shark"), she says "Tyger, tyger, burning bright...". This is a reference to a poem called "[The Tyger](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Tyger "wikipedia:The Tyger")", written by English poet William Blake in 1794.
* Her quote for [Telltale Heart](/wiki/Telltale_Heart "Telltale Heart"), "Your choices matter.", may be a reference to [Telltale Games](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Telltale_Games "wikipedia:Telltale Games") video game company, famous for releasing adventure games where the player's choices (don't) have a significant impact on the story line.
* Her quote for the [Rock Den](/wiki/Rock_Den "Rock Den") ("Oh. The abyss is staring back at me...") may be reference to the works of [Friedrich Nietzsche](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Friedrich_Nietzsche "wikipedia:Friedrich Nietzsche").
* When she examines a [Broodling](/wiki/Broodling "Broodling"), she says "My, what big eyes you have". This is likely a reference to the fairytale *[Little Red Riding Hood](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Little_Red_Riding_Hood "wikipedia:Little Red Riding Hood")*.
  + Her quote for the [Large Ornate Chest](/wiki/Large_Ornate_Chest "Large Ornate Chest") ("My, what magnificent horns you have!") is similar to this.
* Wendy's quote for Wickerbottom as a murderer ("'Murder', she wrote.) is a reference to the [American crime drama](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Murder,_She_Wrote "wikipedia:Murder, She Wrote") of the same name.
* When she examines a [Gnome](/wiki/Trinkets#Gnome "Trinkets"), she says "I'd carry this to the end of the world." This is likely a reference to the gnome found in *[Half Life 2: Episode 2](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Half_Life_2:_Episode_2 "wikipedia:Half Life 2: Episode 2")* that gave an achievement after being from its original location very early on, to the rocket that the player launches in the end of the game.
* When she examines the [Gramaphone](/wiki/Gramaphone "Gramaphone"), she references the Danse Macabre, which is considered to be the "dance between the living and the dead."
* When she examines the [Scaled Furnace](/wiki/Scaled_Furnace "Scaled Furnace"), she references to the childhood story of "Hansel and Gretel" in which the evil witch asks Gretel to see if the furnace is hot enough.
* Her announcement quote for entering light ("And there was light!") is a reference to Genesis 1 from the Bible.
* Her announcement quote for a volcanic eruption in *Shipwrecked* ("Not with a bang, but with an ERUPTION!") is a reference to [T.S. Elliot](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/T._S._Eliot "wikipedia:T. S. Eliot")'s poem *[The Hollow Men](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Hollow_Men "wikipedia:The Hollow Men")*.
* Her quote for the loss of a round in [The Gorge](/wiki/The_Gorge "The Gorge") ("What a horrible place to have a curse.") is a reference to *[Castlevania II: Simon's Quest](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Castlevania_II:_Simon%27s_Quest "wikipedia:Castlevania II: Simon's Quest")*, in which the phrase "What a horrible night to have a curse" displays when day transitions to night.
* Her quotes for Flour ("Flour by any other name would smell as sweet.") and the Sweetish Fish ("A fish, by any name, should not smell sweet." are references to [a phrase](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_rose_by_any_other_name_would_smell_as_sweet "wikipedia:A rose by any other name would smell as sweet") from *Romeo and Juliet*.
* Wendy's examination quote for Appeasing Adornments ("Should old acquaintance be forgot.") is a reference to the Scottish folk song "[Auld Lang Syne](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Auld_Lang_Syne "wikipedia:Auld Lang Syne")".
* Her quote for the Giant Pumpkin ("If only it could become a carriage and carry me far away from here.") may be a reference to certain versions of the [wikipedia:Cinderella](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cinderella "wikipedia:Cinderella") story, where the fairy godmother turns a pumpkin into a carriage for Cinderella.
* Her quote for the Giant Pomegranate ("I wonder how long a single seed would keep one trapped in the underworld...") is a reference to [the abduction of Persephone](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persephone#Abduction_myth "wikipedia:Persephone") from Greek mythology.
